  function sendPageLoadTimeToGA() {
    var performance = window.performance || window.msPerformance || window.webkitPerformance;
    var pageEnd = performance.mark('pageEnd');
      if (!pageEnd || !pageEnd.startTime) {
        return;
      }
      var loadTime = pageEnd.startTime / 1000;
      if (loadTime > 0) {
       window.dataLayer.push({
       event: 'web-vitals',
       event_category: 'Web Vitals',
       event_action: 'pageLoadTime',
       event_value: loadTime
     })
    }
  }
  window.addEventListener('load', function() {
    sendPageLoadTimeToGA();
  });

You can then use the search bar to enter the bus, train, or subway line number or name. Moovit will display the line&#x27;s route, schedule, and real-time arrival information.</p></div></li><li class="qna-item "><button type="button" class="qna-item-trigger" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="qna-answer-1" id="qna-question-1"><div class="qna-item-heading"><img class="qna-item-icon" src="https://appassets.mvtdev.com/index/public-transit-resources/img/question-mark-green.svg" alt="" loading="lazy" height="24" width="24"/><h3 class="qna-item-question">How do I plan a trip using public transit in the app?</h3></div><img class="qna-item-chevron " src="https://appassets.mvtdev.com/index/public-transit-resources/img/chevron-down.svg" alt="" loading="lazy" height="16" width="16"/></button><div id="qna-answer-1" class="qna-item-content " role="region" aria-labelledby="qna-question-1" aria-hidden="true"><p class="qna-item-answer">To plan a trip, open the Moovit app and enter your destination in the &#x27;Where to?&#x27; search bar. The app will show you several route options using local public transit like buses, trains, or subways. You can review the suggested routes, which include travel times and step-by-step directions, to choose the one that works for you.</p></div></li><li class="qna-item "><button type="button" class="qna-item-trigger" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="qna-answer-2" id="qna-question-2"><div class="qna-item-heading"><img class="qna-item-icon" src="https://appassets.mvtdev.com/index/public-transit-resources/img/question-mark-green.svg" alt="" loading="lazy" height="24" width="24"/><h3 class="qna-item-question">How do I check the bus schedule for my line?</h3></div><img class="qna-item-chevron " src="https://appassets.mvtdev.com/index/public-transit-resources/img/chevron-down.svg" alt="" loading="lazy" height="16" width="16"/></button><div id="qna-answer-2" class="qna-item-content " role="region" aria-labelledby="qna-question-2" aria-hidden="true"><p class="qna-item-answer">You can find the schedule for any transit line in the Moovit app by searching for the line number or tapping on a station. From there, you can see upcoming arrival times and select the option to view the full timetable. This allows you to check the bus schedule, train times, and more.</p></div></li></ul></div></div></section><section class="continents-countries-wrapper"><div class="content-wrapper"><div class="continents-title-container"><h1 class="continents-title">Public transit by country</h1></div><div class="continents-list-container"><div class="continent-toggle-item description-country-list">Choose a country/region and discover how to go anywhere with public transit, so you can travel like a local.
